<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отморозить.html>отморо́зить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otmorózitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ок</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отморозок.html>отморо́зок</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otmorózok</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отморозок.html>отморо́зка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отморозок.html>отморо́зки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отморозок.html>отморо́зков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> thug, scumbag, monster <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a person utterly lacking moral scruples</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2002</b>,  Варвара Синицына (Varvara Sinitsyna),  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:муза.html>Му́за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:генерал.html>генера́л</a></cite>  | <cite>The Muse and the General</cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:честный.html>че́стный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бандит.html>банди́т</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отморозок.html>отморо́зок</a></b>. <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>дете́й</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женщина.html>же́нщин</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:инвалид.html>инвали́дов</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:трогать.html>тро́гаю</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja čéstnyj bandít, ne <b>otmorózok</b>. Detéj, žénščin i invalídov ne trógaju.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I'm an honest gangster, not a <b>monster</b>. I don't hurt children, women, and the disabled.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***отмывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отмывать.html>отмыва́ть</a> (25620)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отмыть.html>отмы́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otmýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отмывать.html>отмыва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otmyvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отмыть.html>отмы́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wash clean
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отмывать.html>отмыва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>руки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otmyvátʹ</b> ruki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to wash one's hands clean</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to wash off, to wash away
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отмывать.html>отмыва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:грязь.html>грязь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otmyvátʹ</b> grjazʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to wash off the dirt</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to launder
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отмывать.html>отмыва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́ньги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otmyvátʹ</b> dénʹgi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to launder money</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">отмыва́ние</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otmyvánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>нести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

</p>
<ol><li>to treat (<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">k</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + dative case)</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отнимать.html>отнима́ть</a> (7117)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нима́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nimátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отнимать.html>отнима́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otnimátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отнять.html>отня́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to take (from)</li>
<li>to subtract; to take away; to abstract</li>
<li>to deduct, to take away, to take from, to take off</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">also figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take away (from); to bereave (of)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отнимать.html>отнима́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>неё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:последний.html>после́днюю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надежда.html>наде́жду</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ne <b>otnimáj</b> u nejó poslédnjuju nadéždu.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Don't take away her last hope.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to withdraw; to remove (hands)</li>
<li>to rob (of), to deprive (of)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to amputate</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:относить.html>относи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otnosítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to refer</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹnyj</span>, <span class="ann-pos">verbal adjective suffix</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, perhaps a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">relātīvus</i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:относить.html>относи́ть</a> (7997)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носить.html>носи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:относить.html>относи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otnosítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отнести.html>отнести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to refer</li>
<li>to attribute, to ascribe <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to associate ownership or authorship with</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to relegate</li>
<li>to take</li>
<li>to charge</li>
<li>to appropriate</li>
<li>to take to</li>
<li>to take back</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:относить.html>относи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otnosítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носить.html>носи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wear until worn off or until stopping to wear, to wear for a while</li>
<li>to carry, to bear for a while</li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li>to treat (<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">k</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + dative case)

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to date from</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to apply, to appertain <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to belong to or be a part of, whether by right, nature, appointment, or custom; to relate to</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to concern, to have to do</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:относить.html>относи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otnosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>си́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***отношение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отношение.html>отноше́ние</a> (326)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:относить.html>относи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otnosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отношение.html>отноше́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otnošénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отношение.html>отноше́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отношение.html>отноше́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отношение.html>отноше́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>attitude</li>
<li>treatment</li>
<li>relation, regard, consideration
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отношение.html>отноше́нию</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">po <b>otnošéniju</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">as regards</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́том</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отношение.html>отноше́нии</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v étom <b>otnošénii</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">in this respect</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всех</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отношение.html>отноше́ниях</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vo vsex <b>otnošénijax</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">in every respect</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>други́х</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отношение.html>отноше́ниях</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v drugíx <b>otnošénijax</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">in other respects</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:много.html>мно́гих</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отношение.html>отноше́ниях</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vo mnógix <b>otnošénijax</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">in many respects</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обострять.html>обостря́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отношение.html>отноше́ния</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">obostrjátʹ <b>otnošénija</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to strain <b>relations</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отношение.html>отноше́ниях</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>други́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>людьми́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>otnošénijax</b> s drugími ljudʹmí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in <b>relationships</b> with other people</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>ratio</li>
<li>official letter</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отнять.html>отня́ть</a> (3492)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ня́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-njátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отнять.html>отня́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otnjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отнимать.html>отнима́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">отыма́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to take (from)</li>
<li>to subtract; to take away; to abstract</li>
<li>to deduct, to take away, to take from, to take off</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">also figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take away (from); to bereave (of)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отнять.html>о́тнял</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>неё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:последний.html>после́днюю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надежда.html>наде́жду</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>ótnjal</b> u nejó poslédnjuju nadéždu.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He has taken away her last hope.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to withdraw; to remove (hands)</li>
<li>to rob (of), to deprive (of)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to amputate</li></ol>

***отображать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отображать.html>отобража́ть</a> (30186)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">отобрази́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otobrazítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отображать.html>отобража́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otobražátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">отобрази́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">also  figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to reflect</li>
<li>to depict, to represent, to reproduce</li>
<li>to display</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geometry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to project</li></ol>
